      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font id="TAB1" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 396pt"></font>Exhibit 99.1</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25">&#160;</div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25"><br>&#160;</div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: right" align="left"><img src="acl6k0509wavelightex9910.jpg" alt=""></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25">
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Alcon
Achieves Required Ownership in WaveLight AG to Initiate Squeeze-out</font></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">HUENENBERG, Switzerland &#8211; May 12,
2009</font> &#8211;<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">&#160;</font>Alcon, Inc., (NYSE: ACL)
announced today that the company has achieved ownership of more than 95 percent
of the share capital of WaveLight AG (ISIN: DE0005125603).&#160;&#160;Under the
provisions of the German Stock Corporation Act, Alcon is deemed to be the
principal shareholder of WaveLight&#8217;s approximately 6.6 million issued and
outstanding shares.&#160;&#160;The company has notified the WaveLight board of
directors of its intention to acquire all remaining outstanding shares in
accordance with the &#8220;squeeze-out&#8221; provisions of German securities
law.&#160;&#160;Alcon intends to acquire these remaining shares in exchange for
appropriate cash compensation following the WaveLight annual general meeting to
be held on August 28, 2009.</font></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font id="TAB1" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt"></font>&#8220;Completing the WaveLight acquisition
will enable us to finalize the combination of Alcon&#8217;s global commercial
infrastructure with WaveLight&#8217;s leading technologies,&#8221; said Kevin Buehler,
Alcon&#8217;s president and chief executive officer. &#8220;While we have successfully
integrated our refractive operations in the United States and other selected
markets, we look forward to further market development opportunities and
operating efficiencies afforded by full ownership.&#8221;</font></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"># #
#</font></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">About
Alcon</font></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff">Alcon, Inc. is the world&#8217;s
leading </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">eye
care</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff">company, with sales of
approximately $6.3 billion in 2008. Alcon, which has been dedicated to the
ophthalmic industry for 60 years, researches, develops, manufactures and markets
pharmaceuticals, surgical equipment and devices, contact lens care solutions and
other vision care products that treat diseases, disorders and other conditions
of the eye. Alcon&#8217;s majority shareholder is </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff">Nestl&#233;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff">, </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff">S.A.</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff">, the world&#8217;s largest food
company. For more information on Alcon, Inc., visit the Company&#8217;s web site at
</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">www.alcon.com</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff">.</font></font></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">About
WaveLight AG</font></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">WaveLight
AG develops, manufactures and markets an innovative, end-to-end product
portfolio in the field of ophthalmology, specializing in diagnostic systems and
refractive surgery, including the ALLEGRETTO<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super">&#174;</font> laser
system.&#160;&#160;The ALLEGRETTO WAVE<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super">&#174;</font> Eye-Q
excimer laser combines precision technology with excellent laser energy
stability, high-quality components and reliability.&#160;&#160;Built with
Pioneering wavefront principles, the laser&#8217;s PerfectPulse Technology<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super">&#174;</font> is
designed to control each laser pulse from its generation to the exact point
where it contacts the cornea.</font></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Legal Disclaimer: </font>This press
release is neither an offer to buy nor a request to submit an offer to sell
shares in WaveLight AG.</font></div>
